msg:This is the best hotel in Yanbian area, with luxurious facilities and five-star service standards. The exterior of the hotel is very grand, and at night it looks like a Chinese movie set. There are many places to take pictures, not only during the day, but also at night. A North Korean girl played the piano in the lobby, and the reception staff were efficient and multilingual. The whole hotel is full of Korean cultural characteristics, which made me feel very comfortable. The hotel also has a large parking lot, as well as a luxury shuttle service. The breakfast was very varied and the seating was very comfortable. The room was so large that I felt like I was living in a Korean palace. The ordinary rooms are comparable to the presidential suites in many hotels across the country. I am looking forward to staying at this hotel again. Highly recommend!

When choosing a hotel, I was attracted by the National Garden. Although the place is not as big as Yanji Folk Garden, I feel that the photo effect should be similar to that of the Folk Garden, so I decisively chose to live here. It should be the most luxurious hotel in the area. It is very a**ospheric from the entrance to the lobby. The room facilities are complete and clean. The layout is very folk. The hot water and heating are sufficient. The hotel provides free ethnic costume photography. The a**osphere during the day is gorgeous at night, and the photos are more beautiful. It is very convenient to travel. You can ask the hotel front desk to call a taxi. It is basically 5 yuan to go anywhere in the city, and the most expensive is only 11 yuan to go a little further. It is really cost-effective. The big seafood in Hunchun must be eaten. It is so delicious that I am still swallowing my saliva. And Hunchun basically has what Yanji has. We can make up for Zhengtan fried chicken and Shunji cold noodles that we can't eat in Yanji here, and there is no regret. For this hotel and seafood, I must bring my parents to Hunchun again next year, and I must stay at your house again.
